good meate ſhall doe wel sommer ye ſhall giue braunches tender bruiſe tree ſuch ye get vſe two moneths faſt let feed morning fieldes ſo milke giue alſo euening freſh forrage ſhe commeth houſe likewiſe cattell mē enough ſayeth helpe ſame beeing taken betimes diſeaſe cōmeth infection blood appeareth commonly firſt head head wil ſwell eyne waxe greate wil runne water doe froth mouth hee paſt remedie ſhortly hee dye yet thus ſicke eate remedy yee ſhal flea beaſt ſo dead burie deepe pitte couer wel earth dogges come carrion ſo many beaſtes ſmell thereof like infected ſame diſeaſe therewith yee ſhall ſkinne ſtreight tanner carrie home feare peril maie fall thereof common vſe done great charity put beaſt ſkinne pole ſette hedge faſt bounde ſtake high waye ſide euery man ryding maie perceiue graſſe agayne winter woulde bee put houſes rather remaine abroade giue haye nightes paſture day time thus beyng vſed ſhall bee muche better handle ſhall kine ox ſerue purpoſe loſſe calfe lambe fole couet féed cattell alſo horſe loues feede low groundes plaſhes hollow place horſes ſhéepe ſo well agree together except ſheepe féede vpper groundes ſheepe féed bare paſſure eate ſwéeteſt graſſe ſo horſe likewiſe hee muſt haue longer yet ſome ſay horſe wil eate nigh ground ſheepe cannot therewith fill belly ſo ſoone one hundreth cattell paſture ye may haue xx horſes low ground plenty graſſe ye may put therein hundreth ſhéepe mo ſo likewiſe rate goodnes paſture leſſe cattell order yee maye eate paſtures euen cattell leaue tuftes graſſe vneaten alſo high ground ye may put ſhéep leſſe cattell manye kine draught ox eate ground much barer fatting ox kine ye may alſo giue mylch cowe well much meat little much meate make ſoone fatte ſhee rather take bull ſhee fatte giue leſſer milke leanner cowe fatnes ſtoppeth poares raines ſhould conueigh milke vnto vdderne wherefore meane paſture alwaies beſt keepe mylch kyne haue good meane eſtate neither fatte leane alſo cowe bee fatte ſhee ſhall calue ſhee daunger leane calfe ſhee fatte ſhall leſſe ſtature draught ox yee cannot giue much meate except bee graſſe lowe mowed meddowe cauſe haue gyrrie hee maye away ſo well labour likewiſe much graſſe cloſe cattell feede worſe therof better good ſwéete bitte earth large déepe graſſe long beaſts byte toppes thereof ſweeteſt graſſe ſhall remayne ſtill grounde ſo rotte beaſt eate thereof horſes onely winter féede foggie graſſe ſuch like alſo ye ſhall vnderſtand horſes cattell may well foddered winter together put apart beaſtes horne gore horſes ſhéepe wherefore daunger ſo féede together beſt ſomer winter ſet vp ye take graſſe ſommer hardly fall eating hay good yee take vp kéepe ſo without meat water one daye night ſo extreme hunger forget graſſe rather firſt giue little haye whereby may
